2002 - January 1st - Fare Increase
2002 - July 1st - People Mover initiates 1st phase of Route Restructure, starting Crosstown Route 1, suspending Hillside Routes and eliminating DASH program (Free Downtown Area Short Hop)
2002 - March 17th (Sunday) - operated reduced service (36%) due to 26+ inches of snow - Affected Monthly Average Ridership & Revenue Hours
2002 - March 18th (Monday) - operated reduced service (49%) due to 26+ inches of snow - Affected Monthly Average Ridership & Revenue Hours
2003 - July 7th - 2nd Phase Route Restructure implemented - Saturday & Sunday Service added on Route 1, hourly service to Airport on Route 7
            Memory Headways on Routes 1, 2, 7, 9, 14, 60, 75 on Weekdays, Sat. & Sun. - Memory Headways on Route 45 on Sat. & Sun.
            Added 22.29 Timetable Revenue Hours each Weekday, 34.36 each Saturday and 37.20 each Sunday
2004 - January 1st - Fare Increase
2004 - July 26th - 3rd Phase Route Restructure implemented - Memory Headways on all routes except for Route 45 weekday
            Replaced Routes 11, 12 & 76 with New Routes 13, 15 & 77. Reconfigured Eagle River service and began DART in the Eagle River & Hillside areas
            Added 38.05 Timetable Revenue Hours each Weekday, 12.10 each Saturday and 20.60 each Sunday
2004 - July 26th to September 30 - FREE Service on Route 77          2004 - July 26th to December 31st - FREE Service on DART
2004 - December 24th & 31st - Saturday service operated. On 12/24, trips starting after 8 pm were not operated
2005 - January 1st - Began selling Reduced Fare Day Passes to Seniors and People with Disabilities
2005 - Summer - No Air Show this year is a reason for lower Shuttle Ridership
2005 - October 1st - Fare Increase
2005 - December 24, trips starting after 8 pm were not operated      2005 - December 26 (Monday), Sunday service operated
2006 - January 2 (Monday), Sunday service operated
2006 - February 6 (Monday) - operated reduced weekday service - 302.63 timetable revenue hours. No trips operated between 10 and 3:30 due to extremely icy road conditions
2006 - Summer - No Air Show this year is a reason for lower Shuttle Ridership
2006 - July 10 - Service Change. DART replaced by Routes 77B/77G, 79 and 65. Weekday TTRH decreased by 2.97, Sat. TTRH increased 2.09 & Sun. TTRH increased by 0.37
2006 - October 22-29 - AFN Convention (Free Rides with Pass)
2007 - Summer - No Air Show this year is a reason for lower Shuttle Ridership (Mayor's Marathon and Botancial Gardens Shuttle on same weekend)
2008 - July 21 - Service Change. Weekday TTRH increased by 12.71, Sat TTRH increased by 5.8 & Sun TTRH increased by 4.7. - Routes 65 & 79 eliminated.
        30 min frequencies on Routes 9 & 15, Route 45G (short turn) trips added. Route 77B/G separated into 77 & 78, many trips extended to/from Peters Creek, some changes to 102
